Up2date Registration
====================

Some notes outlining what up2date does for the registration process.
This is from my personal notes, so probably stands for some corrections.

registration.reserve_user()
.new_user()
.new_system()
 Passed a list of one dict
 [{os_release: '4',
   password: 'foobar',
   profile_name: '---',
   release_name: "Fedora-release',
   rhnuuid: "---",
   username: "---",
   uuid: "---"
 }]

.register_product()
 Passed user info:
 [{address1:
   address2:
   city:
   company:
   contact_email: True
   country:
   first_name:
   last_name:
   state:
   zip:
 }]

.add_hw_packages()
 Passed a list of many dicts.  Each dict has at least the 'class' key in 
 common.

.add_packages()
 [[n, v, r, e], ...]

With the extending packageProfile capability:
  [[n, v, r, e, a, 'buildhost stamp'], ...]
